Introduction

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Base URL

http://mage.tech:8899

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Endpoints

GET api/user

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://mage.tech:8899/api/user" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://mage.tech:8899/api/user"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (401):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
access-control-allow-origin: *
 

{
    "message": "Unauthenticated."
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:

GET api/user

GET api/classify

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://mage.tech:8899/api/classify" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://mage.tech:8899/api/classify"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 60
x-ratelimit-remaining: 59
access-control-allow-origin: *
 

[]
Received response:
Request failed with error:

GET api/analyze/{track}

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://mage.tech:8899/api/analyze/officiis" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://mage.tech:8899/api/analyze/officiis"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 60
x-ratelimit-remaining: 58
access-control-allow-origin: *
 

{
    "error": "officiis does not exist , Please upload and try again"
}

Request      

GET api/analyze/{track}

URL Parameters

track  string  

Filters, sorts, and fetches the list of resources.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://mage.tech:8899/api/songs/search" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://mage.tech:8899/api/songs/search"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/songs/search

Creates a batch of new resources in a transaction-safe way.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://mage.tech:8899/api/songs/batch" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"resources\": [
        \"et\"
    ]
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://mage.tech:8899/api/songs/batch"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "resources": [
        "et"
    ]
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/songs/batch

Body Parameters

resources  string[]  

Update a batch of resources in a transaction-safe way.

Example request:
curl --request PATCH \
    "http://mage.tech:8899/api/songs/batch" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"resources\": [
        \"sed\"
    ]
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://mage.tech:8899/api/songs/batch"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "resources": [
        "sed"
    ]
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "PATCH",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

PATCH api/songs/batch

Body Parameters

resources  string[]  

Deletes a batch of resources in a transaction-safe way.

Example request:
curl --request DELETE \
    "http://mage.tech:8899/api/songs/batch" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://mage.tech:8899/api/songs/batch"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "DELETE",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

DELETE api/songs/batch

Fetches the list of resources.

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://mage.tech:8899/api/songs" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://mage.tech:8899/api/songs"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
